I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
[BUG] Kinesis: IncreaseStreamRetentionPeriod with same value should be a no-op (not an error)
## Service

Kinesis

## AWS API Action

`IncreaseStreamRetentionPeriod` — `POST /` with `Action=IncreaseStreamRetentionPeriod`

## Related issue

This is a follow-up to #291 (which added the `IncreaseStreamRetentionPeriod` implementation). The API now exists but its error handling differs from real AWS in an edge case that breaks Terraform.

## Expected behavior (real AWS)

On real AWS, calling `IncreaseStreamRetentionPeriod` with the **same value** as the current retention period is a **no-op** — it returns success without error.

```bash
# Stream already has 24h retention
aws kinesis increase-stream-retention-period \
  --stream-name my-stream \
  --retention-period-hours 24
# ✅ Returns success (no-op)
```

This is important because Terraform calls `IncreaseStreamRetentionPeriod` on every apply when the `retention_period` attribute is set, even if the value hasn't changed.

## Actual behavior (Floci 1.5.2)

Floci returns `InvalidArgumentException` when the requested retention period equals the current retention period:

```
InvalidArgumentException: Requested retention period (24 hours) must be 
greater than current retention period (24 hours)
```

This is technically correct per the API name ("increase"), but it differs from real AWS behavior and causes Terraform to **taint the Kinesis stream resource**. Tainted streams cause cascading failures — dependent resources like Lambda Event Source Mappings fail to create.

### Reproduction

```bash
# Start Floci
docker run -d -p 4566:4566 hectorvent/floci:latest

# Create a Kinesis stream (default retention: 24h)
aws --endpoint-url http://localhost:4566 kinesis create-stream \
  --stream-name test-stream \
  --shard-count 1

# Set retention to 24h (same as default) — this should be a no-op
aws --endpoint-url http://localhost:4566 kinesis increase-stream-retention-period \
  --stream-name test-stream \
  --retention-period-hours 24
# ❌ InvalidArgumentException: Requested retention period (24 hours) must be 
#    greater than current retention period (24 hours)
```

### Terraform context

This specifically affects repos using **nested Terraform modules** where the inner module has a hardcoded default of 24h that can't be overridden from the outer module:

```hcl
# Inner module (infra-terraform shared module)
variable "retention_period" {
  default = 24
}

resource "aws_kinesis_stream" "stream" {
  name             = var.stream_name
  shard_count      = var.shard_count
  retention_period = var.retention_period  # Always 24, can't be set to null
}
```

Terraform output:
```
Error: increasing Kinesis Stream (my-stream) retention period: 
InvalidArgumentException: Requested retention period (24 hours) must be 
greater than current retention period (24 hours)
```

## Impact

- Terraform taints the Kinesis stream resource
- Dependent resources (Lambda ESMs, consumers) fail to create
- `lifecycle { ignore_changes = [retention_period] }` only works when you control the module definition (not possible with shared/nested modules)
- `|| true` absorbs the error but leaves the stream tainted in Terraform state

## Suggested fix

If the requested retention period equals the current retention period, return success (HTTP 200, empty body) instead of `InvalidArgumentException`. This matches real AWS behavior.

## Environment

- Floci version: 1.5.2 (`hectorvent/floci:latest` as of April 2026)
- Terraform AWS provider: v5.x
- Running Floci in Docker Compose

</pr_description>

    47	        String storageKey = regionKey(region, streamName);
    48	        if (store.get(storageKey).isPresent()) {
    49	            throw new AwsException("ResourceInUseException", "Stream already exists: " + streamName, 400);
    50	        }
    51	
    52	        String arn = regionResolver.buildArn("kinesis", region, "stream/" + streamName);

   131	    }

   133	    public Map<String, String> listTagsForStream(String streamName, String region) {
   134	        return resolveStream(streamName, region).getTags();
   135	    }
   136	
   137	    public void startStreamEncryption(String streamName, String encryptionType, String keyId, String region) {
   138	        KinesisStream stream = resolveStream(streamName, region);
   139	        stream.setEncryptionType(encryptionType);
   140	        stream.setKeyId(keyId);
   141	        store.put(regionKey(region, streamName), stream);
   142	    }
   143	
   144	    public void increaseStreamRetentionPeriod(String streamName, int retentionPeriodHours, String region) {
   145	        KinesisStream stream = resolveStream(streamName, region);
   146	        if (retentionPeriodHours > 8760) {
   147	            throw new AwsException("InvalidArgumentException",
   148	                    "Retention period must not exceed 8760 hours (365 days)", 400);
   149	        }
   150	        if (retentionPeriodHours <= stream.getRetentionPeriodHours()) {
   151	            throw new AwsException("InvalidArgumentException",
   152	                    "Requested retention period (" + retentionPeriodHours +
   153	                    " hours) must be greater than current retention period (" +
   154	                    stream.getRetentionPeriodHours() + " hours)", 400);
   155	        }
   156	        stream.setRetentionPeriodHours(retentionPeriodHours);
   157	        store.put(regionKey(region, streamName), stream);
   158	        LOG.infov("Increased retention period for stream {0} to {1} hours", streamName, retentionPeriodHours);
   159	    }
   160	
   161	    public void decreaseStreamRetentionPeriod(String streamName, int retentionPeriodHours, String region) {
   162	        KinesisStream stream = resolveStream(streamName, region);
   163	        if (retentionPeriodHours < 24) {
   164	            throw new AwsException("InvalidArgumentException",
   165	                    "Retention period must not be less than 24 hours", 400);
   166	        }
   167	        if (retentionPeriodHours >= stream.getRetentionPeriodHours()) {
   168	            throw new AwsException("InvalidArgumentException",
   169	                    "Requested retention period (" + retentionPeriodHours +
   170	                    " hours) must be less than current retention period (" +
   171	                    stream.getRetentionPeriodHours() + " hours)", 400);
   172	        }
   173	        stream.setRetentionPeriodHours(retentionPeriodHours);
   174	        store.put(regionKey(region, streamName), stream);
   175	        LOG.infov("Decreased retention period for stream {0} to {1} hours", streamName, retentionPeriodHours);
   176	    }
   177	
   178	    public void stopStreamEncryption(String streamName, String region) {
   179	        KinesisStream stream = resolveStream(streamName, region);
   180	        stream.setEncryptionType("NONE");
   181	        stream.setKeyId(null);
   182	        store.put(regionKey(region, streamName), stream);
   183	    }
   184	
   185	    public void splitShard(String streamName, String shardId, String newStartingHashKey, String region) {
   186	        KinesisStream stream = resolveStream(streamName, region);
   187	        KinesisShard parent = stream.getShards().stream()
   188	                .filter(s -> s.getShardId().equals(shardId))
   189	                .findFirst()
   190	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("ResourceNotFoundException", "Shard " + shardId + " not found", 400));
   191	
   192	        if (parent.isClosed()) {
   193	            throw new AwsException("InvalidArgumentException", "Shard " + shardId + " is already closed", 400);
   194	        }
   195	
   196	        parent.setClosed(true);
   197	        parent.setSequenceNumberRange(new KinesisShard.SequenceNumberRange(
   198	                parent.getSequenceNumberRange().startingSequenceNumber(),
   199	                String.valueOf(sequenceGenerator.get())));
   200	
   201	        String start = parent.getHashKeyRange().startingHashKey();
   202	        String end = parent.getHashKeyRange().endingHashKey();
   203	
   204	        KinesisShard child1 = new KinesisShard(nextShardId(stream), start, subtractOne(newStartingHashKey), String.valueOf(sequenceGenerator.get()));
   205	        child1.setParentShardId(shardId);
   206	
   207	        KinesisShard child2 = new KinesisShard(nextShardId(stream), newStartingHashKey, end, String.valueOf(sequenceGenerator.get()));
   208	        child2.setParentShardId(shardId);
   209	
   210	        stream.getShards().add(child1);
   211	        stream.getShards().add(child2);
   212	        store.put(regionKey(region, streamName), stream);
   213	        LOG.infov("Split shard {0} in stream {1}", shardId, streamName);
   214	    }
   215	
   216	    public void mergeShards(String streamName, String shardId, String adjacentShardId, String region) {
   217	        KinesisStream stream = resolveStream(streamName, region);
   218	        KinesisShard shard1 = stream.getShards().stream()
   219	                .filter(s -> s.getShardId().equals(shardId))
   220	                .findFirst()
   221	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("ResourceNotFoundException", "Shard " + shardId + " not found", 400));
   222	        KinesisShard shard2 = stream.getShards().stream()
   223	                .filter(s -> s.getShardId().equals(adjacentShardId))
   224	                .findFirst()
   225	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("ResourceNotFoundException", "Shard " + adjacentShardId + " not found", 400));
   226	
   227	        if (shard1.isClosed() || shard2.isClosed()) {
   228	            throw new AwsException("InvalidArgumentException", "One or both shards are already closed", 400);
   229	        }

    66	    private String resolveStreamName(JsonNode request) {
    67	        String streamName = request.path("StreamName").asText(null);
    68	        if (streamName != null && !streamName.isBlank()) {
    69	            return streamName;
    70	        }
    71

    74	            int streamIdx = streamArn.indexOf(":stream/");
    75	            if (streamIdx >= 0) {
    76	                String after = streamArn.substring(streamIdx + 8);
    77	                int slash = after.indexOf('/');
    78	                String name = slash >= 0 ? after.substring(0, slash) : after;
    79	                if (!name.isBlank()) {
    80	                    return name;
    81	                }
    82	            }
    83	        }
    84	
    85	        throw new AwsException("InvalidArgumentException",
    86	                "StreamName or valid StreamARN must be provided", 400);
    87	    }

     1	package io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.common;
     2	
     3	import io.github.hectorvent.floci.config.EmulatorConfig;
     4	import jakarta.enterprise.context.ApplicationScoped;
     5	import jakarta.inject.Inject;
     6	import jakarta.ws.rs.core.HttpHeaders;
     7	
     8	import java.util.regex.Matcher;
     9	import java.util.regex.Pattern;
    10	
    11	@ApplicationScoped
    12	public class RegionResolver {
    13	
    14	    // Matches: Credential=AKID/20260215/us-west-2/s3/aws4_request
    15	    private static final Pattern CREDENTIAL_REGION_PATTERN =
    16	            Pattern.compile("Credential=\\S+/\\d{8}/([^/]+)/");
    17	
    18	    private final String defaultRegion;
    19	    private final String defaultAccountId;
    20	
    21	    @Inject
    22	    public RegionResolver(EmulatorConfig config) {
    23	        this(config.defaultRegion(), config.defaultAccountId());
    24	    }
    25	
    26	    public RegionResolver(String defaultRegion, String defaultAccountId) {
    27	        this.defaultRegion = defaultRegion;
    28	        this.defaultAccountId = defaultAccountId;
    29	    }
    30	
    31	    public String resolveRegion(HttpHeaders headers) {
    32	        if (headers == null) {
    33	            return defaultRegion;
    34	        }
    35	        String auth = headers.getHeaderString("Authorization");
    36	        if (auth == null || auth.isEmpty()) {
    37	            return defaultRegion;
    38	        }
    39	        Matcher matcher = CREDENTIAL_REGION_PATTERN.matcher(auth);
    40	        if (matcher.find()) {
    41	            return matcher.group(1);
    42	        }
    43	        return defaultRegion;
    44	    }
    45	
    46	    public String getDefaultRegion() {
    47	        return defaultRegion;
    48	    }
    49	
    50	    public String getAccountId() {
    51	        return defaultAccountId;
    52	    }
    53	
    54	    public String buildArn(String service, String region, String resource) {
    55	        return "arn:aws:" + service + ":" + region + ":" + defaultAccountId + ":" + resource;
    56	    }
    57	}
    58

cat > /tmp/repro_kinesis_retention.sh <<'EOF'
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
cd /testbed
PORT="${PORT:-4566}"
BASE="http://localhost:${PORT}"
LOG="/tmp/floci-repro-${PORT}.log"
rm -f "$LOG"
# Start the already-built app in the background for black-box reproduction.
java -Dquarkus.http.port="$PORT" -jar target/quarkus-app/quarkus-run.jar >"$LOG" 2>&1 &
PID=$!
cleanup() {
  kill "$PID" >/dev/null 2>&1 || true
  wait "$PID" >/dev/null 2>&1 || true
}
trap cleanup EXIT

for i in {1..60}; do
  if curl -sS "$BASE/_localstack/health" >/dev/null 2>&1 || curl -sS "$BASE" >/dev/null 2>&1; then
    break
  fi
  if ! kill -0 "$PID" >/dev/null 2>&1; then
    echo "server exited early" >&2
    cat "$LOG" >&2
    exit 1
  fi
  sleep 1
done

STREAM="retention-repro-$$"
json_post() {
  local action="$1" body="$2"
  curl -sS -i -X POST "$BASE/" \
    -H "Content-Type: application/x-amz-json-1.1" \
    -H "X-Amz-Target: Kinesis_20131202.${action}" \
    -d "$body"
}

create_resp=$(json_post CreateStream "{\"StreamName\":\"$STREAM\",\"ShardCount\":1}")
echo "$create_resp" | head -1
same_resp=$(json_post IncreaseStreamRetentionPeriod "{\"StreamName\":\"$STREAM\",\"RetentionPeriodHours\":24}")
echo "$same_resp"
if echo "$same_resp" | head -1 | grep -q "200"; then
  echo "SAME_RETENTION_NOOP_OK"
else
  echo "SAME_RETENTION_FAILED"
  exit 2
fi
EOF
chmod +x /tmp/repro_kinesis_retention.sh

     9	import java.util.function.Predicate;
    10	
    11	/**
    12	 * Thread-safe in-memory storage backed by ConcurrentHashMap.
    13	 * No persistence — data is lost on shutdown unless explicitly flushed.
    14	 */
    15	public class InMemoryStorage<K, V> implements StorageBackend<K, V> {
    16	
    17	    private final ConcurrentHashMap<K, V> store = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
    18	
    19	    @Override
    20	    public void put(K key, V value) {
    21	        store.put(key, value);
    22	    }
    23	
    24	    @Override
    25	    public Optional<V> get(K key) {
    26	        return Optional.ofNullable(store.get(key));
    27	    }
    28	
    29	    @Override
    30	    public void delete(K key) {
    31	        store.remove(key);
    32	    }
    33	
    34	    @Override
    35	    public List<V> scan(Predicate<K> keyFilter) {
    36	        List<V> result = new ArrayList<>();
    37	        store.forEach((k, v) -> {
    38	            if (keyFilter.test(k)) {
    39	                result.add(v);
    40	            }
    41	        });
    42	        return result;
    43	    }
    44	
    45	    @Override
    46	    public Set<K> keys() {
    47	        return Collections.unmodifiableSet(store.keySet());
    48	    }
    49	
    50	    @Override
    51	    public void flush() {
    52	        // No-op for in-memory storage
    53	    }
    54	
    55	    @Override
    56	    public void load() {
    57	        // No-op for in-memory storage
    58	    }
    59	
    60	    @Override
    61	    public void clear() {
    62	        store.clear();
    63	    }

   344	    private KinesisStream resolveStream(String streamName, String region) {
   345	        return store.get(regionKey(region, streamName))
   346	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("ResourceNotFoundException", "Stream " + streamName + " not found", 400));
   347	    }
   348	
   349	    private KinesisShard selectShard(KinesisStream stream, String partitionKey) {
   350	        // Simple hash-based shard selection among ALL shards, then resolve to open one
   351	        int index = Math.abs(partitionKey.hashCode()) % stream.getShards().size();
   352	        KinesisShard shard = stream.getShards().get(index);
   353	        
   354	        // If closed, find the first open child (simplified)
   355	        while (shard.isClosed()) {
   356	            KinesisShard finalShard = shard;
   357	            shard = stream.getShards().stream()
   358	                    .filter(s -> finalShard.getShardId().equals(s.getParentShardId()) || finalShard.getShardId().equals(s.getAdjacentParentShardId()))
   359	                    .filter(s -> !s.isClosed())
   360	                    .findFirst()
   361	                    .orElse(shard); // Fallback to itself if no open child found
   362	            if (shard == finalShard) break; // prevent infinite loop
   363	        }
   364	        return shard;
   365	    }
   366	
   367	    private String regionKey(String region, String name) {
   368	        return region + "::" + name;
   369	    }

cat > /tmp/repro_kinesis_retention.sh <<'EOF'
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
cd /testbed
JAVA25=/usr/lib/jvm/java-25-openjdk-amd64/bin/java
PORT="${PORT:-4568}"
BASE="http://localhost:${PORT}"
LOG="/tmp/floci-repro-${PORT}.log"
rm -f "$LOG"
(
  cd target/quarkus-app
  "$JAVA25" -Dquarkus.http.port="$PORT" -jar quarkus-run.jar
) >"$LOG" 2>&1 &
PID=$!
cleanup() {
  kill "$PID" >/dev/null 2>&1 || true
  wait "$PID" >/dev/null 2>&1 || true
}
trap cleanup EXIT

ready=0
for i in $(seq 1 60); do
  if curl -sS "$BASE/_localstack/health" >/dev/null 2>&1 || curl -sS -X POST "$BASE/" >/dev/null 2>&1; then
    ready=1
    break
  fi
  if ! kill -0 "$PID" >/dev/null 2>&1; then
    echo "server exited early" >&2
    cat "$LOG" >&2
    exit 1
  fi
  sleep 1
done
if [ "$ready" != 1 ]; then
  echo "server did not become ready" >&2
  cat "$LOG" >&2
  exit 1
fi

STREAM="retention-repro-$$"
json_post() {
  local action="$1" body="$2"
  curl -sS -i -X POST "$BASE/" \
    -H "Content-Type: application/x-amz-json-1.1" \
    -H "X-Amz-Target: Kinesis_20131202.${action}" \
    -d "$body"
}

create_resp=$(json_post CreateStream "{\"StreamName\":\"$STREAM\",\"ShardCount\":1}")
echo "$create_resp" | head -1
same_resp=$(json_post IncreaseStreamRetentionPeriod "{\"StreamName\":\"$STREAM\",\"RetentionPeriodHours\":24}")
echo "$same_resp"
if echo "$same_resp" | head -1 | grep -q "200"; then
  echo "SAME_RETENTION_NOOP_OK"
else
  echo "SAME_RETENTION_FAILED"
  exit 2
fi
EOF
chmod +x /tmp/repro_kinesis_retention.sh
PORT=4568 /tmp/repro_kinesis_retention.sh

+        }
         stream.setRetentionPeriodHours(retentionPeriodHours);
         store.put(regionKey(region, streamName), stream);
         LOG.infov("Increased retention period for stream {0} to {1} hours", streamName, retentionPeriodHours);
